    REL: bugfix release 1.0.5
    
     ### Core
    - `lib/message`: `Report()` can now create a Report instance from Event instances (#1225).
    - `lib/bot`:
      * The first word in the log line `Processed ... messages since last logging.` is now adaptible and set to `Forwarded` in the existing filtering bots (#1237).
      * Kills oneself again after proper shutdown if the bot is XMPP collector or output (#970). Previously these two bots needed two stop commands to get actually stopped.
    - `lib/utils`: log: set the name of the `py.warnings` logger to the bot name (#1184).
    
     ### Bots
     #### Collectors
    - `bots.collectors.mail.collector_mail_url`: handle empty downloaded reports (#988).
    - `bots.collectos.file.collector_file`: handle empty files (#1244).
    
     #### Parsers
    - Shadowserver parser:
      * SSL FREAK: Remove optional column `device_serial` and add several new ones.
      * Fixed HTTP URL parsing for multiple feeds (#1243).
    - Spamhaus CERT parser:
      * add support for `smtpauth`, `l_spamlink`, `pop`, `imap`, `rdp`, `smb`, `iotscan`, `proxyget`, `iotmicrosoftds`, `automatedtest`, `ioturl`, `iotmirai`, `iotcmd`, `iotlogin` and `iotuser` (#1254).
      * fix `extra.destination.local_port` -> `extra.source.local_port`.
    
     #### Experts
    - `bots.experts.filter`: Pre-compile regex at bot initialization.
    
     ### Tests
    - Ensure that the bots did process all messages (#291).
    
     ### Tools
    - `intelmqctl`:
      * `intelmqctl run` has a new parameter `-l` `--loglevel` to overwrite the log level for the run (#1075).
      * `intelmqctl run [bot-id] mesage send` can now send report messages (#1077).
    - `intelmqdump`:
      * has now command completion for bot names, actions and queue names in interacive console.
      * automatically converts messages from events to reports if the queue the message is being restored to is the source queue of a parser (#1225).
      * is now capable to read messages in dumps that are dictionaries as opposed to serialized dicts as strings and does not convert them in the show command (#1256).
      * truncated messages are no longer used/saved to the file after being shown (#1255).
      * now again denies recovery of dumps if the corresponding bot is running. The check was broken (#1258).
      * now sorts the dump by the time of the dump. Previously, the list was in random order (#1020).
    
     ### Known issues
    no known issues

    REL: bugfix release 1.0.5
    
     ### Core
    - `lib/message`: `Report()` can now create a Report instance from Event instances (#1225).
    - `lib/bot`:
      * The first word in the log line `Processed ... messages since last logging.` is now adaptible and set to `Forwarded` in the existing filtering bots (#1237).
      * Kills oneself again after proper shutdown if the bot is XMPP collector or output (#970). Previously these two bots needed two stop commands to get actually stopped.
    - `lib/utils`: log: set the name of the `py.warnings` logger to the bot name (#1184).
    
     ### Bots
     #### Collectors
    - `bots.collectors.mail.collector_mail_url`: handle empty downloaded reports (#988).
    - `bots.collectos.file.collector_file`: handle empty files (#1244).
    
     #### Parsers
    - Shadowserver parser:
      * SSL FREAK: Remove optional column `device_serial` and add several new ones.
      * Fixed HTTP URL parsing for multiple feeds (#1243).
    - Spamhaus CERT parser:
      * add support for `smtpauth`, `l_spamlink`, `pop`, `imap`, `rdp`, `smb`, `iotscan`, `proxyget`, `iotmicrosoftds`, `automatedtest`, `ioturl`, `iotmirai`, `iotcmd`, `iotlogin` and `iotuser` (#1254).
      * fix `extra.destination.local_port` -> `extra.source.local_port`.
    
     #### Experts
    - `bots.experts.filter`: Pre-compile regex at bot initialization.
    
     ### Tests
    - Ensure that the bots did process all messages (#291).
    
     ### Tools
    - `intelmqctl`:
      * `intelmqctl run` has a new parameter `-l` `--loglevel` to overwrite the log level for the run (#1075).
      * `intelmqctl run [bot-id] mesage send` can now send report messages (#1077).
    - `intelmqdump`:
      * has now command completion for bot names, actions and queue names in interacive console.
      * automatically converts messages from events to reports if the queue the message is being restored to is the source queue of a parser (#1225).
      * is now capable to read messages in dumps that are dictionaries as opposed to serialized dicts as strings and does not convert them in the show command (#1256).
      * truncated messages are no longer used/saved to the file after being shown (#1255).
      * now again denies recovery of dumps if the corresponding bot is running. The check was broken (#1258).
      * now sorts the dump by the time of the dump. Previously, the list was in random order (#1020).
    
     ### Known issues
    no known issues

    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Introduction of the Enabled-Switch for Collectors.
    
    This introduces the enabled-switch for all Collector-Bots.
    By doing so it fixes #715.
    
    The Collectorbot was extended with an own start-function
    which checks if the enabled paramter is present and was set
    to a representation of False. To check the "representation of
    False" the function to_bool was introduced in utils.py, which
    maps well-known-text to booleans. It has a a fallbackmode parameter
    which determines if the function returns true of false if no
    mapping  was found.
    
    As long as to_bool does not evaluate to False the bot will be started.

    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    REL: bugfix release 1.0.5
    
     ### Core
    - `lib/message`: `Report()` can now create a Report instance from Event instances (#1225).
    - `lib/bot`:
      * The first word in the log line `Processed ... messages since last logging.` is now adaptible and set to `Forwarded` in the existing filtering bots (#1237).
      * Kills oneself again after proper shutdown if the bot is XMPP collector or output (#970). Previously these two bots needed two stop commands to get actually stopped.
    - `lib/utils`: log: set the name of the `py.warnings` logger to the bot name (#1184).
    
     ### Bots
     #### Collectors
    - `bots.collectors.mail.collector_mail_url`: handle empty downloaded reports (#988).
    - `bots.collectos.file.collector_file`: handle empty files (#1244).
    
     #### Parsers
    - Shadowserver parser:
      * SSL FREAK: Remove optional column `device_serial` and add several new ones.
      * Fixed HTTP URL parsing for multiple feeds (#1243).
    - Spamhaus CERT parser:
      * add support for `smtpauth`, `l_spamlink`, `pop`, `imap`, `rdp`, `smb`, `iotscan`, `proxyget`, `iotmicrosoftds`, `automatedtest`, `ioturl`, `iotmirai`, `iotcmd`, `iotlogin` and `iotuser` (#1254).
      * fix `extra.destination.local_port` -> `extra.source.local_port`.
    
     #### Experts
    - `bots.experts.filter`: Pre-compile regex at bot initialization.
    
     ### Tests
    - Ensure that the bots did process all messages (#291).
    
     ### Tools
    - `intelmqctl`:
      * `intelmqctl run` has a new parameter `-l` `--loglevel` to overwrite the log level for the run (#1075).
      * `intelmqctl run [bot-id] mesage send` can now send report messages (#1077).
    - `intelmqdump`:
      * has now command completion for bot names, actions and queue names in interacive console.
      * automatically converts messages from events to reports if the queue the message is being restored to is the source queue of a parser (#1225).
      * is now capable to read messages in dumps that are dictionaries as opposed to serialized dicts as strings and does not convert them in the show command (#1256).
      * truncated messages are no longer used/saved to the file after being shown (#1255).
      * now again denies recovery of dumps if the corresponding bot is running. The check was broken (#1258).
      * now sorts the dump by the time of the dump. Previously, the list was in random order (#1020).
    
     ### Known issues
    no known issues

    intelmq_psql_initdb.py JSON instead of String
    
    Modified the file in order to create database columns of type
    json instead of string.
    This enhances the processing speed of data which is stored in the
    extras column.
    
    ATTENTION: This is a schema-alteration of the EventDB.
    If data already exists in the EventDB it might be required, that data is
    converted from string to json.
    Refer to: http://www.postgresql.org/docs/9.2/static/datatype-json.html
    
    This change requires a PostgreSQL 9.2 or higher.

    bug in 32a291e60b28d4f38a2692b02a1c06aa49faa436
    debug instance has also PID file
    additional log error message
    background process gets paused, hint for exiting console, reverting errors
    error in the bot shouldnt affect whole botnet
    
    We had an error – our proprietary bot wasn't listed in BOTS file. Thus, no launcher in bin was created. When launching whole botnet only bots that preceded this bot in the alphabet were launched, the rest stayed stopped.
    With this change, when an error occurs, the rest of the botnet will stay unaffected → only erroneous bots won't get launched → it will be easier to detect the bug for the administrator.

    ENH: ctl: non-blocking bot/net reload
    
    first reload all bots, then check their status
    follow-up of be4eca1838781283844564e395150cc5fe82281e
    non-blocking bot/net starting/stopping
    
    Until now, when starting or stopping a bot, we had to wait 0.25 sec. Intelmqctl waited for the bot to load and checked if it loaded properly.
    Problems:
    * When having 100 bots, we have to wait 25 s only to start the botnet.
    * 0.25 s sometimes isn't enough: The bot seemed to be started without problem... than it immediately crashed due to an error, but in intelmq-manager, we saw that it was running till browser reload. It is so frustrating!
    
    I've rewritten the class so that we wait 0.5 s whether we are starting/stopping a single bot or a whole botnet. (There is a new keyword parameter "getstatus" that handles that.)
    This seems to work very well. I'd be glad if you add this to the code.

    Former-commit-id: 6bccfa86ab49c91a8628ea90bda9788c11665819
    ENH: intelmqctl logs to file and add stream logger
    
    intelmqctl has a log file as requested in certtools/intelmq#218 (partial fix)
    To achieve this, the logger got extended by a stream handler aside the existing file handler. This helps debugging bots as running them solely on the console, directly gives the log output in stderr (default of StreamHandler)
    
    
    Former-commit-id: e681b57321ec8c4a6b945c671bbbc164ca4bad0d
    ENH: intelmqctl log parsing/reading simplified
    
    The logs are read and parsed backwards, which is more efficient than reading and parsing the entire file from the beginning
    The code to read the file is easier to read and understand now, however some code in utils reads the file backwards in chunks.
    This change is currently not compatible with intelmq-manager as it wants to read the line number which is not read anymore as its not possible to get it by reading the file backwards. Yet a line number does not make sense in log files.

    ENH: bot tests check class name and event fields
    
    It is checked if the Bot class has a CamelCase name
    and ends with CollectorBot, ParserBot etc.
    
    It the bot is a parser or expert, it will be checked if the
    event has some essential fields like feed.url or raw.
    Same applies to collectors.
    
    bot_id is 'test-bot' by default, but can be changed.

    alpha release
    FIX: Removed IP-Address REGEX from Generic CSV-Parser
    
    This fixes https://github.com/certtools/intelmq/issues/855
    temporarily by removing the broken regex.
    
    Nevertheless, this BREAKS the funtionality of grabbing IP's from
    strings such as "192.168.5.1:80".
    
    IF YOUR FEEDS CONTAIN SUCH DATA, DO NOT APPLY THIS FIX ON YOUR
    PRODUCTIVE SYSTEM, WITHOUT CHANGING YOUR FEEDS FIRST!
    TST: Ignore __name__ branch for coverage

    ENH: bot tests check class name and event fields
    
    It is checked if the Bot class has a CamelCase name
    and ends with CollectorBot, ParserBot etc.
    
    It the bot is a parser or expert, it will be checked if the
    event has some essential fields like feed.url or raw.
    Same applies to collectors.
    
    bot_id is 'test-bot' by default, but can be changed.

    TST: msg: add test with hardcoded hash
    
    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Do not copy the message to compute the hash in the deduplicator
    
    This improves the speed of the deduplicator substantially because, as it
    turns out, it spent much of its time when actually processing events
    copying the message just to be able to remove the keys that should be
    ignored in the hash.
    
    To avoid that copy, the message's hash method now takes an additional,
    optional parameter with a set of keys that should be ignored and the
    deduplicator uses that parameter instead of modifying a copy of the
    message.
    
    Fixes #613 (at least it improves speed substantially)
    TST: lib/msg hierarchical made optional
    
    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    BUG: harm: loosen constraints on hashes

    we can use unittest.mock and remove the requirement for an external mock.

    BUG+TST: Fix encoding issues
    
    fixes #278
    fixes #281
    
    I hope all problems are solved now. Short summary:
    it often happened that decode was called on an unicode string, which resulted in an implicit encoding
        and the other way round -> total mess
    sometimes the utils functions were called, then the string functions itself
    encoding is now strictly separated: unicode in all bots and bytes in all pipelines. No one except
        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    ENH: bot tests check class name and event fields
    
    It is checked if the Bot class has a CamelCase name
    and ends with CollectorBot, ParserBot etc.
    
    It the bot is a parser or expert, it will be checked if the
    event has some essential fields like feed.url or raw.

        and the other way round -> total mess

        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    we can use unittest.mock and remove the requirement for an external mock.

    This amends commit 1b0bef96d801d28dd075cbd9679e10d76aefa164, somehow two files
    were not pushed...
    
    It is now possible to:
     1) Connect to a server using username / password
     2) Receive messages which were send to the bot directly
     3) Receive messages which were send in a room
     All Messages are send into the MessageQueue without further
     processing.
    
    the room must be configured in format:
     room@server.example.com
    
    I added a __init__.py to be able to load the bot as module.
    
    The bot was tested briefly with sleekxmpp 1.0-beta5.
    It responded as expected to direct messages and messages in rooms.
     - The use of password-protected rooms was not tested.

    Former-commit-id: c8cf294ef59e27bfb81b09d88252c376fe6ba828
    Add bot for Microsoft DCU feed
    
    This commit adds a first version of the Microsoft DCU Collector.
    What does this bot do? It opens a remote azure account which contains
    feed data from the Digital Crime Unit (DCU) and sents it into the
    IntelMQ system.
    
    Options for the bot:
      azure_account_name -- a valid name of an azure account
      azure_account_key  -- a valid key for that azure account
      delete             -- a flag, if set true it will delete the
                            remote blob and container. (Not yet tested)
      date               -- a relative date for selecting a container
                            (Not yet tested)
    
    The bot is based on:
    https://github.com/adulau/dcu-tools

    Reworked the XMPP-Collector:
    
     - Renamed xmpp-Client
     - Made Stop more robust (at least I hope so)
    Added Stop Method to Collector Bot
    Added a JSON Parser bot to read a JSON String
    
     - Convert the JSON String into an Event
     - Adapted the XMPP Collector.
    Integrated comments of Sebix and reformatted code.
    Extended the XMPPCollectorBot
    
     * Do not use a function called send_message in XMPPClientBot
       as it is hard to follow if XMPP's send_message or IntelMQ's
       send_message function is used
    The XMPP Bot is now capable to connect to a rom on an XMPP Server.
    
    This amends commit 1b0bef96d801d28dd075cbd9679e10d76aefa164, somehow two files
    were not pushed...
    
    It is now possible to:
     1) Connect to a server using username / password
     2) Receive messages which were send to the bot directly
     3) Receive messages which were send in a room
     All Messages are send into the MessageQueue without further
     processing.
    
    the room must be configured in format:
     room@server.example.com
    
    I added a __init__.py to be able to load the bot as module.
    
    The bot was tested briefly with sleekxmpp 1.0-beta5.
    It responded as expected to direct messages and messages in rooms.
     - The use of password-protected rooms was not tested.

    Add code for XMPP bots
    
    This includes the code for both the collector and the output bots.
    Code is based on the example in PRs 158 and 197.
    DOC: typosquatting with aspell in bots/
    Extended and corrected documentation of XMPP-Bots
    XMPP: Enhanced the XMPP Output and Collector.
    
     - Added Readmes
     - Collector can use a whitelist/blacklist to ignore certain users
     - Output can use MUC in better way.
    Added the possibility to configure Multi-User-Chat
    
    The XMPP Bot is now capable to connect to a rom on an XMPP Server.
    
    It is now possible to:
     1) Connect to a server using username / password
     2) Receive messages which were send to the bot directly
     3) Receive messages which were send in a room
     All Messages are send into the MessageQueue without further
     processing.
    
    the room must be configured in format:
     room@server.example.com
    
    I added a __init__.py to be able to load the bot as module.
    
    The bot was tested briefly with sleekxmpp 1.0-beta5.
    It responded as expected to direct messages and messages in rooms.
     - The use of password-protected rooms was not tested.

    Mail collectors: explicitly close IMAP connection
    
    This patch adds an explicit mailbox.close() command to end the IMAP
    connection.  Without this, mail does not get marked as \Seen reliably.
    Optionally split large inputs in mail URL collector bot
    
    The mail URL collector bot now has two new parameters, chunk_size and
    chunk_replicate_header, controlling whether the input is to be split
    into chunks and how big those chunks should be and what to do with (CSV)
    header lines.
    
    Part of issue #547
    ENH: mail collector: remove unnecessary strips
    
    Introduced by f14b8acbe671532311f519f7cbb66be0f796e9bc
    
    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Strip certain characters from URLs
    
    This removes the following characters from URLs:
    
            - leading and trailing spaces
            - newlines and carriage returns
    
    This should help prevent unexpected behavior, e.g., when configuring
    a URL regex such as 'http://.*'.
    Always convert mail body to string
    
    Imbox presents mail bodies as byte strings at times.  While it's not
    clear under which circumstances Imbox does this, this patch simply
    always converts the body to string format.
    Only mark msgs as read if they match the configured patterns
    
    Assuming that multiple instances of the mail collector bot can watch the
    same mailbox, an instance should probably only mark messages as read
    that it is "responsible for".

    find . -name '*.py' | xargs sed -i 's/from intelmq.lib.bot import Bot, sys/import sys\nfrom intelmq.lib.bot import Bot/'

    BUG+TST: Fix encoding issues
    
    fixes #278
    fixes #281
    
    I hope all problems are solved now. Short summary:
    it often happened that decode was called on an unicode string, which resulted in an implicit encoding
        and the other way round -> total mess
    sometimes the utils functions were called, then the string functions itself
    encoding is now strictly separated: unicode in all bots and bytes in all pipelines. No one except
        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    FIX: Removed IP-Address REGEX from Generic CSV-Parser

    temporarily by removing the broken regex.

    strings such as "192.168.5.1:80".

    PRODUCTIVE SYSTEM, WITHOUT CHANGING YOUR FEEDS FIRST!

    Log a warning if required fields could not be found
    
    This partially fixes #744 (1, 2) by adding a warning
    to the log to indicate that the dataformat sent by shadowserver
    might have changed.
    
    In addition this commit fixes the pep8 issue in the config
    and removes the logging of values which could not be added
    to an IntelMQ-DHO field.
    Fixed Log-message
    Downgraded logging in Shadowserver parser.
    
    This commit contains two changes
     1. The loglevel was downgraded to DEBUG when a value could not
        be inserted into an IntelMQ-DHO field, but was added to
        extras instead.
        This happens quite often for the url, cc_geo, cc_dns
        fields in botnet_drone_hadoop configuration.
        Keeping the loglevel at INFO would have blown up the
        logfiles without need.
     2. Enhanced the configuration of the botnet_drone_hadoop
        parser in order to "guess" the destination.url from
        the hostname and url field of the shadowserver data.

    protocol.transport is always tcp for Sinkhole-HTTP-Drone
    
    The transport is implicit in the feed's semantics: It's always about
    HTTP, so "protocol.transport" will always be "tcp" even though the feed
    does not contain this information explicitly.
    
    Implementing this requires a new mechanism that allows a feed
    configuration to specify constant field values.

    Updated the config: Make less assumptions.
    
    As discussed with sebix on irx, we should not make assumptions
    on the protocol. If we have sufficient data to reconstruct the
    url, (irc, http, https is given in application, and hostname and/or url are
    present) we can assume the full destination.url.

    Downgraded logging in Shadowserver parser.
    
    This commit contains two changes
     1. The loglevel was downgraded to DEBUG when a value could not
        be inserted into an IntelMQ-DHO field, but was added to
        extras instead.
        This happens quite often for the url, cc_geo, cc_dns
        fields in botnet_drone_hadoop configuration.
        Keeping the loglevel at INFO would have blown up the
        logfiles without need.
     2. Enhanced the configuration of the botnet_drone_hadoop
        parser in order to "guess" the destination.url from
        the hostname and url field of the shadowserver data.

    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Do not copy the message to compute the hash in the deduplicator
    
    This improves the speed of the deduplicator substantially because, as it
    turns out, it spent much of its time when actually processing events
    copying the message just to be able to remove the keys that should be
    ignored in the hash.
    
    To avoid that copy, the message's hash method now takes an additional,
    optional parameter with a set of keys that should be ignored and the
    deduplicator uses that parameter instead of modifying a copy of the
    message.
    
    Fixes #613 (at least it improves speed substantially)
    Use the full sha256 hash in the deduplicator bot. Fixes #658
    
    The deduplicator bot now uses the full sha256 hash as keys in the cache
    database. Before it would end up using only 64 bits derived from the
    sha256 hash due to using Python's built-in hash function which limits
    hash values to a platform int, i.e. 64 bits on 64 bit platforms. See
    issue #658 for details.
    
    In order to be able to use the sha256 hash, this commit extracts the
    actual computation of the hash of a message from the __hash__ method
    into the new method hash and calls this new method from __hash__ for
    compatibility. The new method returns the full sha256 hash value.
    MAINT: Cleanup bots code, remove unnecessary checks etc.

    BUG+TST: Fix encoding issues
    
    fixes #278
    fixes #281
    
    I hope all problems are solved now. Short summary:
    it often happened that decode was called on an unicode string, which resulted in an implicit encoding
        and the other way round -> total mess
    sometimes the utils functions were called, then the string functions itself
    encoding is now strictly separated: unicode in all bots and bytes in all pipelines. No one except
        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    Modify bot: fix for acces to regex match results.
    
    The second call to apply_action() was missing the parameter 'matches'.
    * Added a default value to the function definition.
    * Assuming a default_condition could also be used to match something
      added the resulting 'matches' to the default call to apply_action().
    Allow modify bot replacement rules to access regex match results.
    
    The replacement rules for the modify bot can now access the results of
    the regex matches that were performed when the event was matched to the
    rules. This allows for more complex replacements because the
    replacements can refer to e.g. regex groups to extract parts of other
    fields. See the change in morefeeds.conf for an example.
    
    In this form the change is somewhat experimental, but it demonstrates
    the principle as well as some of the complications like having to wrap
    the match results to give them a dict-like interface that can be used
    from the format replacement fields.
    BUG: modify: fix rule matching
    
    due to a bug, not all parts of a rule needed to match

    Corrected the rule SecurityScorecard/securityscorecard in morefeeds.conf
    and added a simple unit test for it.
    Modify Bot: improved example and unit test.
    
    Removed morefeeds.conf default.__default action because it was
    interfering with other rules. This was the case because all sections
    will be considered, but in undefined order.
    
    For example when running the bitdefender unittest:
    Depending on which section was executed first,
    the value of classification.identifier was different, because malware.name
    was already modified by the bitdefender rule or not when the
    default.__default action was executed.
    Allow modify bot replacement rules to access regex match results.

    the regex matches that were performed when the event was matched to the
    rules. This allows for more complex replacements because the
    replacements can refer to e.g. regex groups to extract parts of other
    fields. See the change in morefeeds.conf for an example.
    
    In this form the change is somewhat experimental, but it demonstrates
    the principle as well as some of the complications like having to wrap
    the match results to give them a dict-like interface that can be used
    from the format replacement fields.

    BUG+TST: Fix encoding issues

    fixes #281
    
    I hope all problems are solved now. Short summary:
    it often happened that decode was called on an unicode string, which resulted in an implicit encoding
        and the other way round -> total mess
    sometimes the utils functions were called, then the string functions itself
    encoding is now strictly separated: unicode in all bots and bytes in all pipelines. No one except
        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    TESTS: (minor) cleanup: Using unittest.mock now.
    
    mock is now part of the Python standard library, available as
    unittest.mock in Python 3.3 onwards. As we require python3.3,
    we can use unittest.mock and remove the requirement for an external mock.

    BUG+TST: Fix encoding issues
    
    fixes #278
    fixes #281
    
    I hope all problems are solved now. Short summary:
    it often happened that decode was called on an unicode string, which resulted in an implicit encoding
        and the other way round -> total mess
    sometimes the utils functions were called, then the string functions itself
    encoding is now strictly separated: unicode in all bots and bytes in all pipelines. No one except
        utils, harmonization, message and pipeline is allowed to do conversions!

    certtools/intelmq#267
    
    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Introduction of the Enabled-Switch for Collectors.
    
    This introduces the enabled-switch for all Collector-Bots.
    By doing so it fixes #715.
    
    The Collectorbot was extended with an own start-function
    which checks if the enabled paramter is present and was set
    to a representation of False. To check the "representation of
    False" the function to_bool was introduced in utils.py, which
    maps well-known-text to booleans. It has a a fallbackmode parameter
    which determines if the function returns true of false if no
    mapping  was found.
    
    As long as to_bool does not evaluate to False the bot will be started.

    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Automatically copy feed.provider to the Event if present
    Do not copy the message to compute the hash in the deduplicator
    
    This improves the speed of the deduplicator substantially because, as it
    turns out, it spent much of its time when actually processing events
    copying the message just to be able to remove the keys that should be
    ignored in the hash.
    
    To avoid that copy, the message's hash method now takes an additional,
    optional parameter with a set of keys that should be ignored and the
    deduplicator uses that parameter instead of modifying a copy of the
    message.
    
    Fixes #613 (at least it improves speed substantially)
    Use the full sha256 hash in the deduplicator bot. Fixes #658
    
    The deduplicator bot now uses the full sha256 hash as keys in the cache
    database. Before it would end up using only 64 bits derived from the
    sha256 hash due to using Python's built-in hash function which limits
    hash values to a platform int, i.e. 64 bits on 64 bit platforms. See
    issue #658 for details.
    
    In order to be able to use the sha256 hash, this commit extracts the
    actual computation of the hash of a message from the __hash__ method
    into the new method hash and calls this new method from __hash__ for
    compatibility. The new method returns the full sha256 hash value.

    Signed-off-by: Sebastian Wagner <sebix@sebix.at>
    Introduction of the Enabled-Switch for Collectors.
    
    This introduces the enabled-switch for all Collector-Bots.
    By doing so it fixes #715.
    
    The Collectorbot was extended with an own start-function
    which checks if the enabled paramter is present and was set
    to a representation of False. To check the "representation of
    False" the function to_bool was introduced in utils.py, which
    maps well-known-text to booleans. It has a a fallbackmode parameter
    which determines if the function returns true of false if no
    mapping  was found.
    
    As long as to_bool does not evaluate to False the bot will be started.

    ENH: intelmqctl logs to file and add stream logger

    Former-commit-id: e681b57321ec8c4a6b945c671bbbc164ca4bad0d
    ENH: intelmqctl log parsing/reading simplified
    
    The logs are read and parsed backwards, which is more efficient than reading and parsing the entire file from the beginning
    The code to read the file is easier to read and understand now, however some code in utils reads the file backwards in chunks.
    This change is currently not compatible with intelmq-manager as it wants to read the line number which is not read anymore as its not possible to get it by reading the file backwards. Yet a line number does not make sense in log files.
